TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

2745

NOTICES
MARS CONDUCTORS (INDIA) PRIVATE LIMITED
Manufacturer of Super Enamelled Copper Wire.
Regd. Offi: 102, N.S.C. Bose Road, Chennai-600 079.
FORM No. 155
(See Rule 329)
Members winding up
Notice convening final Meeting.
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a General Meeting of the Members of the above named company
will be held on Wednesday, 31st day of October 2012 at 1/1, Krishnama Road, Nungambakkam, Chennai-600 034 at 11.00
A.M. for the purpose of having an account laid before the members showing them the manner in which the winding up has
been conducted and the property of the company disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may be given by the
liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the company, the manner in which the books, accounts and
documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.

Chennai, 25th October 2012.

CHAIN RAJ JAIN,
Liquidator.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, Muthuselvan, born as a male child to MR. Puthiyavan, born on 18th August 1984, residing at Thangamman Kovil Street,
Kalkurichi, Palamadai Post, Tirunelveli. After the biological change due to an elaborate sexural reassignment surgery she
has been reared as a female (Reference Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, Mch... MNAMS... DIB... N.B. Phd... FICS) KILPAUK MEDICAL
COLLEGE & HOSPITAL, Chennai-600 010.
The Clinical Examination under the reference above also shows that, I Could be reared as a female. Hence,
I, Muthuselvan, shall henceforth be known as M. SELVIMANOJ PREM KUMAR.
Tirunelveli, 25th October 2012.

MUTHUSELVAN.
